    0.8611, 0.9512, 1.0681, 0.9797, 0.8440, 1.0961, 10000.0000, 0.8106, 0.8106, 0.8106,
    0.8106, 0.8105, 0.8106, 0.8193, 0.8106, 0.8106, 0.8107, 0.8106, 0.8192, 0.8106,
    0.8107, 0.8106, 0.8106, 0.8105, 0.8105, 0.8189, 0.8189, 0.8189, 0.8107, 0.8106,
    0.8106, 0.8105, 1.3557, 0.8107, 0.8189, 0.8190, 0.8106, 0.8189, 0.8107, 0.8188
]

# Get the maximum value of the values that are less than 10000
max_value = max([v for v in values if v < 10000])

# Replace the 10000 values by this maximum value
values = [v if v < 10000 else max_value for v in values]

# Number of calls
calls = list(range(1, len(values) + 1))

# Plot the graph
plt.figure(figsize=(10, 5))
plt.plot(calls, values)
plt.xlabel('Number of Calls')
plt.ylabel('min RMSE')
plt.grid(True)
